He was murdered!\r\n\r\nTravel with Pearl to her family home on the Polynesian island of Artemis and help her find clues as well as piece together the puzzles, revealing the truth about mysterious secret orders locked in a struggle to determine the rise and fall of nations. Join our heroine as she unveils the hidden story of deception and betrayal that involves nearly everyone she has ever known or loved. Stand beside her as she seeks and finds hidden strength.
